<Review>The concept of dining in the dark forces you to interact with your fellow guests in a way that would be otherwise socially awkward.

Flavors are more intense, your appreciation for texture, sound and smells are intensified. It's an all around trip for the senses. And the food is delicious to boot.

No strong opinions on the plate presentation or dining room decor.< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics><Resp>None<//Resp><Gmap_id>0x80c2bb4bb0a0a8b1:0x371d2ff4aacc30da<//Gmap_id></record>

<Text>It's definitely an experience to try. They are not lying, the dining room is pitch black, you can't see anything! This was a bit unsettling at first and initially I felt quite anxious but I soon relaxed and grew more and more accustomed to the dark as the meal went on. Eating with silverware was not as difficult as I imagined either and I quickly got use to eating with a fork in the dark. I didn't poke my eye out and I didn't drop and food in my lap.
I was worried that the food might not be that good and the place would be relying mostly on the gimmick of the darkness, but my girlfriend and I both had excellent meals. I would go back, but next time I want to go back and next time go in a big group.<//Text>< Pictures>

<rating>4< /rating>< text>
This is just off of the trail. There are large grassy areas, playground equipment, shade trees, and shelters. The shelters are reserved in advance and the weekends can be busy. Just stop by to kick a soccer ball or play in the equipment. The bathrooms are public and can be clean or bad - depends in the users and their willingness to be respectful.  The trail connected is a good path for walks, runs, or rides. Bicyclists should yield to those walking.< /text>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Picked up a load of batteries here the other day. They loaded them carefully in the truck and even tied them down for us (using our straps). These are very heavy, about 120 pounds each, so you wouldn't be surprised if people loading them were dropping them the last couple inches- not the case here. You'd have thought these guys were loading them up for delivery to their own house!
For the competitive price you get, I think this is a lot smarter than buying online where whoever is shipping it doesn't care about being gentle with ridiculously heavy items like this. You don't want your batteries having a rough shipping trip in my mind. Better to pick them up yourself from people like this who treated them carefully.</review>
